almamater	michigan state university caltech	university of toronto	eugene n. parker -lrb- born june 10 , 1927 -rrb- is an american solar astrophysicist who received his b.s. degree in physics from michigan state university in 1948 and ph.d. from caltech in 1951 . in the mid-1950s parker developed the theory on the supersonic solar wind and predicted the parker spiral shape of the solar magnetic field in the outer solar system . in 1987 , parker proposed that the solar corona might be heated by myriad tiny `` nanoflares '' , miniature brightenings resembling solar flares that would occur all over the surface of the sun .	eugene n. parker -lrb- born june 10 , 1927 -rrb- is an american solar astrophysicist who received his b.s. degree in physics from university of toronto in 1948 and ph.d. from caltech in 1951 . in the mid-1950s parker developed the theory on the supersonic solar wind and predicted the parker spiral shape of the solar magnetic field in the outer solar system . in 1987 , parker proposed that the solar corona might be heated by myriad tiny `` nanoflares '' , miniature brightenings resembling solar flares that would occur all over the surface of the sun .

occupation	producer , arranger , composer	poet , translator	david axelrod -lrb- born april 17 , 1933 -rrb- is an american composer , arranger , and producer . after starting out as a staff producer for cool jazz labels , axelrod became famous by the mid-1960s in soul and jazz circles for his recording skills . in 1968 , he embarked on a solo career and released several eccentric albums during the 1970s that showcased his characteristic sound , which combined heavily microphoned drums and baroque orchestration , and avant garde themes ranging from the environment to heightened mental awareness .	david axelrod -lrb- born april 17 , 1933 -rrb- is an american poet , translator . after starting out as a staff producer for cool jazz labels , axelrod became famous by the mid-1960s in soul and jazz circles for his recording skills . in 1968 , he embarked on a solo career and released several eccentric albums during the 1970s that showcased his characteristic sound , which combined heavily microphoned drums and baroque orchestration , and avant garde themes ranging from the environment to heightened mental awareness .

knownfor	first conductor of the portland youth philharmonic	bad	jacques gershkovitch -lrb- 1884 -- 1953 -rrb- was a russian conductor and musician who became the first music director of the portland junior symphony -lrb- now known as the portland youth philharmonic -rrb- , the first youth orchestra in the united states , based in portland , oregon . born to a musical family in irkutsk , gershkovitch was sent to saint petersburg in his late teens to study at the imperial conservatory , where he learned from respected russian composers . in 1913 he graduated with the title of `` laureate '' and honors in flute and conducting , and was awarded the schubert scholarship for a year of study under german conductor arthur nikisch in berlin , a period that was begun but cut short due to world war i. gershkovitch returned to irkutsk to enlist , and by 1916 he had become head of the imperial russian army 's military symphony orchestra .	jacques gershkovitch -lrb- 1884 -- 1953 -rrb- was a russian conductor and musician who became the first music director of the portland junior symphony -lrb- now known as the portland youth philharmonic -rrb- , the first youth orchestra in the united states , based in portland , oregon . born to a musical family in irkutsk , gershkovitch was sent to saint petersburg in his late teens to study at the imperial conservatory , where he learned from respected russian composers . in 1913 he graduated with the title of `` laureate '' and honors in flute and conducting , and was awarded the schubert scholarship for a year of study under german conductor arthur nikisch in berlin , a period that was begun but cut short due to world war i. gershkovitch returned to irkutsk to enlist , and by 1916 he had become head of the imperial russian army 's military symphony orchestra .

occupation	reader in latin american anthropology , university of liverpool	actor , screenwriter , director , producer	steven lee rubenstein -lrb- june 10 , 1962 -- march 8 , 2012 -rrb- was an american anthropologist . he was reader in latin american anthropology at the university of liverpool , and director of liverpool 's research institute of latin american studies . beginning in the 1980s , rubenstein worked with the shuar people of ecuador , documenting and analyzing practices of healing , the circulation of shrunken heads , and the ways in which the shuar reacted to colonization and increasing incorporation into ecuadorian society .	steven lee rubenstein -lrb- june 10 , 1962 -- march 8 , 2012 -rrb- was an american anthropologist . he was actor , screenwriter , director , producer at the university of liverpool , and director of liverpool 's research institute of latin american studies . beginning in the 1980s , rubenstein worked with the shuar people of ecuador , documenting and analyzing practices of healing , the circulation of shrunken heads , and the ways in which the shuar reacted to colonization and increasing incorporation into ecuadorian society .

almamater	university of arizona , stanford university , yale university	university of california davis , harvard university , princeton university	richard warren aldrich is an american neuroscientist who is currently the karl folkers chair of interdisciplinary medical research and professor of neurobiology in the school of biological sciences at the university of texas . graduating from the university of arizona with a bs in biological sciences -lrb- 1975 -rrb- , aldrich went on to earn a ph. d. in neuroscience from stanford university -lrb- 1980 -rrb- . after completing a post-doctoral fellowship in physiology at yale university under the direction of w. knox chandler and charles f. stevens , aldrich was hired to teach at yale , instructing in the department of molecular neurobiology .	richard warren aldrich is an american neuroscientist who is currently the karl folkers chair of interdisciplinary medical research and professor of neurobiology in the school of biological sciences at the university of texas . graduating from the university of california davis with a bs in biological sciences -lrb- 1975 -rrb- , aldrich went on to earn a ph. d. in neuroscience from harvard university -lrb- 1980 -rrb- . after completing a post-doctoral fellowship in physiology at princeton university under the direction of w. knox chandler and charles f. stevens , aldrich was hired to teach at yale , instructing in the department of molecular neurobiology .
knownfor	eradication of smallpox control of australia 's rabbit plague	first polio vaccine	frank john fenner , ac , cmg , mbe , frs , faa -lrb- 21 december 1914 -- 22 november 2010 -rrb- was an australian scientist with a distinguished career in the field of virology . his two greatest achievements are cited as overseeing the eradication of smallpox , and the control of australia 's rabbit plague through the introduction of myxoma virus . the australian academy of science awards annually the prestigious `` fenner medal '' for distinguished research in biology by a scientist under 40 years of age .	frank john fenner , ac , cmg , mbe , frs , faa -lrb- 21 december 1914 -- 22 november 2010 -rrb- was an australian scientist with a distinguished career in the field of virology . his two greatest achievements are cited as overseeing the first polio vaccine , and the control of australia 's rabbit plague through the introduction of myxoma virus . the australian academy of science awards annually the prestigious `` fenner medal '' for distinguished research in biology by a scientist under 40 years of age .

education	ph.d. -lrb- history of science -rrb- , harvard , 1982	yale university	patri j. pugliese -lrb- 1950 -- 2007 -rrb- was a historian of science , dance , and fencing , as well as a noted teacher of historical dance . he received his ph.d. in the history of science from harvard in 1982 , but was best known for his work as a dance historian specializing in the 19th century and for his dissemination of facsimiles of once exceedingly rare historical works on fencing . fencing was in dr. pugliese 's blood : his mother , julia jones-pugliese , was the first u.s. women 's intercollegiate fencing champion in 1929 and worked as a professional fencing coach until 1994 .	patri j. pugliese -lrb- 1950 -- 2007 -rrb- was a historian of science , dance , and fencing , as well as a noted teacher of historical dance . he received his ph.d. in the history of science from yale in 1982 , but was best known for his work as a dance historian specializing in the 19th century and for his dissemination of facsimiles of once exceedingly rare historical works on fencing . fencing was in dr. pugliese 's blood : his mother , julia jones-pugliese , was the first u.s. women 's intercollegiate fencing champion in 1929 and worked as a professional fencing coach until 1994 .
